src/policies/provider-policy.ts (updated)

Testing:
Vitest

Electron Style:
CommonJS

Application Style:
TypeScript

Rules:

- Reuse existing IPC handlers
- Reuse existing preload bridge
- Never use Jest
- Never assume file paths
- Verify exports before creating tests

=========================================================
SPRINT 28 ARCHITECTURE CHANGES
=========================================================

**Changed Paths (Architecture-affecting):**

- src/llm/\*\* ✓ (gateway.ts, routing-explainer.ts)
- src/policies/\*\* ✓ (policy-presets.ts, sensitive-task-rules.ts, provider-policy.ts)
- electron-ui/preload.cjs ✓ (providerPolicy namespace expanded)
- electron-ui/ipc/\*\* ✓ (provider-policy-handlers.cjs added)
- src/ui/types.d.ts ✓ (Window.providerPolicy updated)

**Service Layer Additions (T1):**

- src/policies/policy-presets.ts: POLICY_PRESETS object, listPolicyPresets(), getPolicyPreset(), isPolicyPresetName(), getAllProviders()
- src/policies/sensitive-task-rules.ts: RULES array (pii, credentials, finance, legal, security), detectSensitiveTask(request) returns { matched, reasons, detectedTypes, forceLocal, approvedProvidersOnly }

**Service Layer Updates (T2):**

- src/policies/provider-policy.ts: imports sensitive-task-rules, applyPolicyPreset(name), applyPolicyToCandidatesWithReason(candidates, request) returns { candidates, policyReason }
- src/llm/gateway.ts: imports applyPolicyToCandidatesWithReason, destructures policyResult, passes policyReason to explainRoutingSelection
- src/llm/routing-explainer.ts: imports detectSensitiveTask, handles sensitive.forceLocal and sensitive rule contexts in explanations

**IPC & Preload Updates (T3):**

- electron-ui/ipc/provider-policy-handlers.cjs: new handlers (listPresets, applyPreset) via ipcMain
- electron-ui/preload.cjs: providerPolicy namespace now includes listPresets() and applyPreset(name)
- src/ui/types.d.ts: Window.providerPolicy extended with listPresets and applyPreset signatures
- src/ui/provider-dashboard.html: preset selector UI + sensitive rules panel

**CLI Updates (T4):**

- src/cli/llm-policy.ts: llm:policy:presets and llm:policy:preset <name> commands added

**Entry Points:** Unchanged (cli.js, main.cjs unchanged)
**IPC Wiring:** CHANGED (new provider-policy-handlers.cjs must be registered in main.cjs)
**Service Structure:** EXTENDED (policy layer now includes presets + sensitivity rules)
**Routing Logic:** EXTENDED (applyPolicyToCandidatesWithReason returns { candidates, policyReason })

**Architecture Impact:** MODERATE

- Adds policy preset framework (5 presets: default, coding, research, private, enterprise)
- Adds sensitive task detection (PII/credentials force local; finance/legal/security restrict providers)
- Extends gateway routing to honor policy presets and sensitive rules
- Extends IPC with policy preset control
- Dashboard and CLI gain preset controls

**Next Sprint Hooks:**

- Workspace memory store per-workspace policy overrides
- Context injection into gateway requests
